## §1 — Iter-1 P1+P2 disposition

| Iter-1 finding | Iter-2 fix |
|---|---|
| **P1** Hand-rolled 1% tolerance differs from canonical `tolerance_for(dim)`; example narrative_length 1055 vs 1000/900 wrongly published BEAT-BOTH instead of BEAT-ONE. | **FIXED.** Imports `tolerance_for` from `src.polaris_graph.audit_ir.beat_both_scoring` and uses it for all BEAT-BOTH/TIE/BEHIND classifications. New regression test `test_canonical_tolerance_used_not_hand_rolled` exercises Codex's exact example (1055 vs 1000/900) and asserts BEAT-ONE. |
| **P2** Missing all-zero N/A guard; structurally unmeasurable dimensions became TIE. | **FIXED.** Mirrors `scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py:492-494` — when polaris_mean=chatgpt=gemini=0, verdict is N/A with rationale "All 3 manifests scored 0.0 — dimension not measurable". New regression test `test_all_zero_dimension_returns_na_not_tie`. |

+"""I-bug-107 — aggregate N BEAT-BOTH runs into mean ± stddev per dimension.
+
+A single BEAT-BOTH run has high variance (sweep-to-sweep recovery rates
+differ ±5pp on identical input due to LLM nondeterminism). For
+benchmark publication and Carney-grade quality reporting, average N
+runs and report mean ± stddev per dimension.
+
+This script does NOT run sweeps — sweep orchestration is user-budget
+gated (each full sweep is ~$0.10 OpenRouter spend). It aggregates
+N pre-existing `outputs/m_live_2_beat_both/manifest.json` artifacts
+that were produced by separate `scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py`
+invocations.
+
+Usage:
+    python scripts/aggregate_beat_both_runs.py \\
+        --manifest path/to/run1/manifest.json \\
+        --manifest path/to/run2/manifest.json \\
+        --manifest path/to/run3/manifest.json \\
+        --output outputs/m_live_2_aggregate/manifest.json
+
+Output schema (mirrors single-run schema with aggregate fields):
+    {
+        "n_runs": 3,
+        "input_manifests": [path1, path2, path3],
+        "polaris_scores_aggregate": {
+            "<dimension>": {
+                "mean": float,
+                "stddev": float,
+                "min": float,
+                "max": float,
+                "values": [v1, v2, v3]
+            }
+        },
+        "chatgpt_scores": {...},     # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
+        "gemini_scores": {...},      # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
+        "per_dimension_verdicts": {
+            "<dimension>": {
+                "polaris_mean": float,
+                "polaris_stddev": float,
+                "chatgpt": float,
+                "gemini": float,
+                "verdict": "BEAT-BOTH" | "BEAT-ONE" | "TIE" | "BEHIND",
+                "robust": bool   # True if (mean - stddev) > both competitors
+            }
+        }
+    }
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import statistics
+import sys
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
+if str(REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
+    sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT))
+
+# I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: reuse canonical per-dimension tolerance
+# from scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py / beat_both_scoring.py instead
+# of a hand-rolled 1% relative tolerance. Canonical tolerance reflects
+# domain knowledge per dimension (narrative_length tolerance is much
+# wider than e.g. unique_citations).
+from src.polaris_graph.audit_ir.beat_both_scoring import (  # noqa: E402
+    tolerance_for,
+)
+
+
+def _load_manifest(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    """Load a single BEAT-BOTH manifest. Validates the expected schema."""
+    if not path.exists():
+        raise FileNotFoundError(f"manifest not found: {path}")
+    data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    required = {"polaris_scores", "chatgpt_scores", "gemini_scores"}
+    missing = required - set(data.keys())
+    if missing:
+        raise ValueError(
+            f"manifest {path} missing required keys: {sorted(missing)}"
+        )
+    return data
+
+
+def _extract_polaris_dimension_values(
+    manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, list[float]]:
+    """Group polaris_scores values by dimension across N manifests.
+
+    Returns: {dimension_name: [run1_value, run2_value, ...]}
+    """
+    by_dim: dict[str, list[float]] = {}
+    for manifest in manifests:
+        for dim_name, dim_score in manifest["polaris_scores"].items():
+            value = dim_score.get("value")
+            if value is None:
+                continue
+            by_dim.setdefault(dim_name, []).append(float(value))
+    return by_dim
+
+
+def _aggregate_polaris_scores(
+    manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
+    """Compute per-dimension mean / stddev / min / max across N runs."""
+    by_dim = _extract_polaris_dimension_values(manifests)
+    aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
+    for dim_name, values in by_dim.items():
+        if not values:
+            continue
+        mean = statistics.mean(values)
+        stddev = statistics.stdev(values) if len(values) >= 2 else 0.0
+        aggregate[dim_name] = {
+            "mean": round(mean, 4),
+            "stddev": round(stddev, 4),
+            "min": min(values),
+            "max": max(values),
+            "values": values,
+            "n": len(values),
+        }
+    return aggregate
+
+
+def _compute_robust_verdicts(
+    polaris_aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
+    chatgpt_scores: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
+    gemini_scores: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
+    """Per-dimension verdict using mean ± stddev for robustness.
+
+    A verdict is "robust BEAT-BOTH" iff (mean - stddev) > both
+    competitor scores (i.e., even the worst-case run beats both).
+
+    Otherwise the verdict uses the mean directly with the original
+    BEAT-BOTH / BEAT-ONE / TIE / BEHIND taxonomy.
+    """
+    verdicts: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
+    for dim_name, agg in polaris_aggregate.items():
+        polaris_mean = agg["mean"]
+        polaris_stddev = agg["stddev"]
+        # I-bug-107 iter-1 P2 fix: explicitly handle missing competitor
+        # dimensions instead of fabricating 0.0. If either competitor
+        # didn't score this dimension, the verdict can't be computed.
+        chatgpt_score = chatgpt_scores.get(dim_name)
+        gemini_score = gemini_scores.get(dim_name)
+        if chatgpt_score is None or gemini_score is None:
+            verdicts[dim_name] = {
+                "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
+                "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
+                "polaris_worst_case": round(polaris_mean - polaris_stddev, 4),
+                "chatgpt": None,
+                "gemini": None,
+                "verdict": "INCOMPLETE",
+                "robust": False,
+                "reason": (
+                    f"competitor missing dimension: "
+                    f"chatgpt={chatgpt_score is None}, "
+                    f"gemini={gemini_score is None}"
+                ),
+            }
+            continue
+        chatgpt_val = chatgpt_score.get("value", 0.0)
+        gemini_val = gemini_score.get("value", 0.0)
+
+        # I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P2 fix: canonical all-zero N/A guard
+        # (mirrors scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py:492-494). When all
+        # three scored 0.0, the dimension is structurally unmeasurable
+        # — emit N/A, not TIE.
+        if polaris_mean == 0.0 and chatgpt_val == 0.0 and gemini_val == 0.0:
+            verdicts[dim_name] = {
+                "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
+                "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
+                "polaris_worst_case": round(polaris_mean - polaris_stddev, 4),
+                "chatgpt": chatgpt_val,
+                "gemini": gemini_val,
+                "verdict": "N/A",
+                "robust": False,
+                "rationale": (
+                    "All 3 manifests scored 0.0 — dimension not "
+                    "measurable on current inputs."
+                ),
+            }
+            continue
+
+        # I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: use canonical per-dimension
+        # tolerance (`tolerance_for(dim)`) — same as the single-run
+        # verdict path. NOT a hand-rolled 1% rule.
+        tol = tolerance_for(dim_name)
+
+        beats_chatgpt = polaris_mean > chatgpt_val + tol
+        beats_gemini = polaris_mean > gemini_val + tol
+        ties_chatgpt = abs(polaris_mean - chatgpt_val) <= tol
+        ties_gemini = abs(polaris_mean - gemini_val) <= tol
+
+        if beats_chatgpt and beats_gemini:
+            verdict = "BEAT-BOTH"
+        elif beats_chatgpt or beats_gemini:
+            verdict = "BEAT-ONE"
+        elif ties_chatgpt and ties_gemini:
+            verdict = "TIE"
+        else:
+            verdict = "BEHIND"
+
+        # I-bug-107 iter-1 P1 fix: robust = STRICT (mean - stddev) > both
+        # competitor scores. NO tolerance — acceptance specifies strict
+        # inequality. A near-margin worst_case=100.5 vs competitor=100
+        # MUST count as robust=True.
+        worst_case = polaris_mean - polaris_stddev
+        robust = worst_case > chatgpt_val and worst_case > gemini_val
+
+        verdicts[dim_name] = {
+            "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
+            "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
+            "polaris_worst_case": round(worst_case, 4),
+            "chatgpt": chatgpt_val,
+            "gemini": gemini_val,
+            "verdict": verdict,
+            "robust": robust,
+        }
+    return verdicts
+
+
+def aggregate(manifest_paths: list[Path], output_path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    """Aggregate N BEAT-BOTH manifests into mean ± stddev per dimension.
+
+    Returns the aggregate manifest dict. Also writes it to output_path.
+    """
+    if len(manifest_paths) < 2:
+        raise ValueError(
+            f"Need >=2 manifests to compute mean ± stddev; got {len(manifest_paths)}"
+        )
+    manifests = [_load_manifest(p) for p in manifest_paths]
+    polaris_aggregate = _aggregate_polaris_scores(manifests)
+
+    # Competitor scores should be identical across runs (same source text).
+    # Use first manifest's scores as the canonical baseline.
+    first = manifests[0]
+    aggregate_manifest = {
+        "milestone": "I-bug-107",
+        "version": "v1",
+        "n_runs": len(manifests),
+        "input_manifests": [str(p) for p in manifest_paths],
+        "polaris_scores_aggregate": polaris_aggregate,
+        "chatgpt_scores": first["chatgpt_scores"],
+        "gemini_scores": first["gemini_scores"],
+        "per_dimension_verdicts": _compute_robust_verdicts(
+            polaris_aggregate,
+            first["chatgpt_scores"],
+            first["gemini_scores"],
+        ),
+        "summary": _build_summary(polaris_aggregate),
+    }
+    output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
+    output_path.write_text(
+        json.dumps(aggregate_manifest, indent=2),
+        encoding="utf-8",
+    )
+    return aggregate_manifest
+
+
+def _build_summary(
+    polaris_aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    """Bird's-eye summary: total dims, dims with high stddev (>10%), etc."""
+    n_dims = len(polaris_aggregate)
+    high_variance_dims = [
+        dim
+        for dim, agg in polaris_aggregate.items()
+        if agg["mean"] != 0 and (agg["stddev"] / abs(agg["mean"])) > 0.1
+    ]
+    return {
+        "n_dimensions": n_dims,
+        "high_variance_dimensions": high_variance_dims,
+        "high_variance_count": len(high_variance_dims),
+    }
+
+
+def main() -> int:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
+        description=__doc__,
+        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--manifest",
+        action="append",
+        required=True,
+        type=Path,
+        help="Path to a BEAT-BOTH manifest.json. Repeatable; >=2 required.",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--output",
+        type=Path,
+        default=Path("outputs/m_live_2_aggregate/manifest.json"),
+        help="Path to write aggregate manifest.",
+    )
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    try:
+        result = aggregate(args.manifest, args.output)
+    except (FileNotFoundError, ValueError) as exc:
+        print(f"ERROR: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
+        return 1
+
+    print(f"Aggregated {result['n_runs']} runs → {args.output}")
+    print(f"  {result['summary']['n_dimensions']} dimensions analyzed")
+    print(
+        f"  {result['summary']['high_variance_count']} high-variance "
+        f"dims (stddev > 10% of mean): "
+        f"{result['summary']['high_variance_dimensions']}"
+    )
+    return 0
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    sys.exit(main())

+"""Tests for I-bug-107 — multi-run BEAT-BOTH aggregator."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+import sys
+from pathlib import Path
+
+import pytest
+
+REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
+if str(REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
+    sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT))
+
+from scripts.aggregate_beat_both_runs import (  # noqa: E402
+    _aggregate_polaris_scores,
+    _compute_robust_verdicts,
+    aggregate,
+)
+
+
+def _make_fake_manifest(polaris_value: float, dim: str = "narrative_length") -> dict:
+    """Synthetic single-run BEAT-BOTH manifest matching real schema."""
+    return {
+        "polaris_scores": {
+            dim: {"value": polaris_value, "higher_is_better": True, "rationale": "test"},
+        },
+        "chatgpt_scores": {
+            dim: {"value": 100.0, "higher_is_better": True, "rationale": "baseline"},
+        },
+        "gemini_scores": {
+            dim: {"value": 90.0, "higher_is_better": True, "rationale": "baseline"},
+        },
+    }
+
+
+def _write(tmp: Path, name: str, manifest: dict) -> Path:
+    p = tmp / name
+    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
+    p.write_text(json.dumps(manifest), encoding="utf-8")
+    return p
+
+
+def test_aggregate_computes_mean_and_stddev(tmp_path: Path):
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(50.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(60.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r3/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(70.0)),
+    ]
+    out = tmp_path / "agg/manifest.json"
+    result = aggregate(paths, out)
+
+    agg = result["polaris_scores_aggregate"]["narrative_length"]
+    assert agg["mean"] == pytest.approx(60.0)
+    assert agg["stddev"] == pytest.approx(10.0)
+    assert agg["min"] == 50.0
+    assert agg["max"] == 70.0
+    assert agg["n"] == 3
+
+
+def test_aggregate_writes_output_file(tmp_path: Path):
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(50.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(60.0)),
+    ]
+    out = tmp_path / "agg/manifest.json"
+    aggregate(paths, out)
+    assert out.exists()
+    written = json.loads(out.read_text())
+    assert written["n_runs"] == 2
+
+
+def test_aggregate_requires_at_least_two_manifests(tmp_path: Path):
+    paths = [_write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(50.0))]
+    with pytest.raises(ValueError, match="Need >=2"):
+        aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+
+
+def test_robust_verdict_when_worst_case_beats_both(tmp_path: Path):
+    """If (mean - stddev) > both competitor scores, verdict is robust.
+
+    Uses canonical narrative_length tolerance (100.0). Values chosen so
+    polaris_mean comfortably exceeds tolerance over both competitors.
+    """
+    # POLARIS: mean=400, stddev=10 → worst_case=390. Competitors 100/90.
+    # 400 > 100+100=200 ✓, 400 > 90+100=190 ✓ → BEAT-BOTH.
+    # 390 > 100 ✓, 390 > 90 ✓ → robust=True (strict).
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(390.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(400.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r3/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(410.0)),
+    ]
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    assert verdict["verdict"] == "BEAT-BOTH"
+    assert verdict["robust"] is True
+
+
+def test_non_robust_verdict_when_high_variance(tmp_path: Path):
+    """If (mean - stddev) does NOT beat both, robust=False even if mean does.
+
+    Under canonical narrative_length tolerance (100.0), polaris_mean must
+    exceed (chatgpt + 100) and (gemini + 100) for BEAT-BOTH. Use values
+    where mean meets the tolerance bar but worst_case (mean - stddev)
+    ties or undercuts a competitor.
+    """
+    # POLARIS: mean=210, stddev=120 → worst_case=90. ChatGPT 100, Gemini 90.
+    # 210 > 100+100=200 ✓ (just), 210 > 90+100=190 ✓ → BEAT-BOTH.
+    # worst_case=90 NOT > chatgpt(100) → robust=False.
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(90.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(210.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r3/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(330.0)),
+    ]
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    assert verdict["verdict"] == "BEAT-BOTH"  # mean (210) > comps + tolerance
+    assert verdict["robust"] is False  # but worst_case (90) does not beat chatgpt (100)
+
+
+def test_canonical_tolerance_used_not_hand_rolled(tmp_path: Path):
+    """I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: tolerance is `tolerance_for(dim)`,
+    not a 1% hand-rolled rule. narrative_length tolerance is 100.0.
+
+    Codex example: narrative_length 1055 vs ChatGPT 1000 / Gemini 900.
+    Under 1% rule (~10 word tolerance): BEAT-BOTH.
+    Under canonical 100-word tolerance: TIE with ChatGPT (only beats Gemini).
+    Verdict should be BEAT-ONE (beats Gemini, ties ChatGPT).
+    """
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(1050.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(1060.0)),
+    ]
+    for p in paths:
+        m = json.loads(p.read_text())
+        m["chatgpt_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 1000.0
+        m["gemini_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 900.0
+        p.write_text(json.dumps(m))
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    # mean=1055 vs chatgpt=1000 (delta=55, < 100 tol → ties); vs gemini=900 (delta=155, > 100 → beats)
+    assert verdict["verdict"] == "BEAT-ONE", (
+        f"canonical tolerance must classify near-margin BEAT-ONE, got {verdict}"
+    )
+
+
+def test_all_zero_dimension_returns_na_not_tie(tmp_path: Path):
+    """I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P2 fix: when all 3 manifests scored 0.0,
+    verdict is N/A (not TIE) — matches canonical M-LIVE-2 logic at
+    scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py:492-494.
+    """
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(0.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(0.0)),
+    ]
+    for p in paths:
+        m = json.loads(p.read_text())
+        m["chatgpt_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 0.0
+        m["gemini_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 0.0
+        p.write_text(json.dumps(m))
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    assert verdict["verdict"] == "N/A"
+    assert verdict["robust"] is False
+
+
+def test_summary_flags_high_variance_dimensions(tmp_path: Path):
+    """Dimensions with stddev > 10% of mean are flagged as high-variance."""
+    # mean=60, stddev=10 → 16.7% — flagged
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(50.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(60.0)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r3/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(70.0)),
+    ]
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    assert "narrative_length" in result["summary"]["high_variance_dimensions"]
+
+
+def test_robust_strict_inequality_no_tolerance(tmp_path: Path):
+    """I-bug-107 iter-1 P1 fix: robust uses STRICT (worst_case > both),
+    NOT tolerance-based comparison. Codex flagged: mean=101, stddev=0.5,
+    competitors=100/99 → worst_case=100.5 > both → robust=True.
+    """
+    # Need 2+ runs to compute stddev; pick values with mean=101, stddev=~0.5
+    # 100.5, 101.5 → mean=101, stddev=0.7071...
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(100.5)),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", _make_fake_manifest(101.5)),
+    ]
+    # Override competitor scores: chatgpt=100, gemini=99
+    for p in paths:
+        m = json.loads(p.read_text())
+        m["chatgpt_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 100.0
+        m["gemini_scores"]["narrative_length"]["value"] = 99.0
+        p.write_text(json.dumps(m))
+
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    # mean=101, stddev~0.71 → worst_case~100.29 > 100 → True; > 99 → True
+    assert verdict["robust"] is True, (
+        f"strict-inequality robust: worst_case={verdict['polaris_worst_case']} "
+        f"vs chatgpt=100, gemini=99 → must be True"
+    )
+
+
+def test_incomplete_verdict_when_competitor_dimension_missing(tmp_path: Path):
+    """I-bug-107 iter-1 P2 fix: if a competitor manifest is missing a
+    dimension, verdict is INCOMPLETE — NOT silently fabricated as 0.0.
+    """
+    m = _make_fake_manifest(50.0, dim="narrative_length")
+    # Remove dim from chatgpt scores entirely
+    del m["chatgpt_scores"]["narrative_length"]
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", m),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", m),
+    ]
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    verdict = result["per_dimension_verdicts"]["narrative_length"]
+    assert verdict["verdict"] == "INCOMPLETE"
+    assert verdict["robust"] is False
+    assert verdict["chatgpt"] is None
+    assert "reason" in verdict
+
+
+def test_aggregate_handles_missing_dimension_gracefully(tmp_path: Path):
+    """If one run is missing a dimension, the aggregate uses only the runs that have it."""
+    m1 = _make_fake_manifest(50.0, dim="narrative_length")
+    m2 = _make_fake_manifest(60.0, dim="narrative_length")
+    # m3 has different dimension
+    m3 = _make_fake_manifest(100.0, dim="other_dim")
+    m3["chatgpt_scores"] = {"other_dim": {"value": 200.0, "higher_is_better": True, "rationale": "x"}}
+    m3["gemini_scores"] = {"other_dim": {"value": 180.0, "higher_is_better": True, "rationale": "x"}}
+    paths = [
+        _write(tmp_path, "r1/manifest.json", m1),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r2/manifest.json", m2),
+        _write(tmp_path, "r3/manifest.json", m3),
+    ]
+    result = aggregate(paths, tmp_path / "agg.json")
+    # narrative_length seen in 2 runs
+    assert result["polaris_scores_aggregate"]["narrative_length"]["n"] == 2
+    # other_dim seen in 1 run — has 1 value, stddev=0 (single sample)
+    assert result["polaris_scores_aggregate"]["other_dim"]["n"] == 1
+    assert result["polaris_scores_aggregate"]["other_dim"]["stddev"] == 0.0

   1: """I-bug-107 — aggregate N BEAT-BOTH runs into mean ± stddev per dimension.
   2: 
   3: A single BEAT-BOTH run has high variance (sweep-to-sweep recovery rates
   4: differ ±5pp on identical input due to LLM nondeterminism). For
   5: benchmark publication and Carney-grade quality reporting, average N
   6: runs and report mean ± stddev per dimension.
   7: 
   8: This script does NOT run sweeps — sweep orchestration is user-budget
   9: gated (each full sweep is ~$0.10 OpenRouter spend). It aggregates
  10: N pre-existing `outputs/m_live_2_beat_both/manifest.json` artifacts
  11: that were produced by separate `scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py`
  12: invocations.
  13: 
  14: Usage:
  15:     python scripts/aggregate_beat_both_runs.py \\
  16:         --manifest path/to/run1/manifest.json \\
  17:         --manifest path/to/run2/manifest.json \\
  18:         --manifest path/to/run3/manifest.json \\
  19:         --output outputs/m_live_2_aggregate/manifest.json
  20: 
  21: Output schema (mirrors single-run schema with aggregate fields):
  22:     {
  23:         "n_runs": 3,
  24:         "input_manifests": [path1, path2, path3],
  25:         "polaris_scores_aggregate": {
  26:             "<dimension>": {
  27:                 "mean": float,
  28:                 "stddev": float,
  29:                 "min": float,
  30:                 "max": float,
  31:                 "values": [v1, v2, v3]
  32:             }
  33:         },
  34:         "chatgpt_scores": {...},     # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
  35:         "gemini_scores": {...},      # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
  36:         "per_dimension_verdicts": {
  37:             "<dimension>": {
  38:                 "polaris_mean": float,
  39:                 "polaris_stddev": float,
  40:                 "chatgpt": float,
  41:                 "gemini": float,
  42:                 "verdict": "BEAT-BOTH" | "BEAT-ONE" | "TIE" | "BEHIND",
  43:                 "robust": bool   # True if (mean - stddev) > both competitors
  44:             }
  45:         }
  46:     }
  47: """

  50:

  52: import json
  53: import statistics
  54: import sys

  56: from typing import Any

  59: if str(REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
  60:     sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT))

  62: # I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: reuse canonical per-dimension tolerance
  63: # from scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py / beat_both_scoring.py instead

  65: # domain knowledge per dimension (narrative_length tolerance is much
  66: # wider than e.g. unique_citations).

  72: def _load_manifest(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
  73:     """Load a single BEAT-BOTH manifest. Validates the expected schema."""
  74:     if not path.exists():
  75:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"manifest not found: {path}")
  76:     data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  77:     required = {"polaris_scores", "chatgpt_scores", "gemini_scores"}
  78:     missing = required - set(data.keys())
  79:     if missing:
  80:         raise ValueError(
  81:             f"manifest {path} missing required keys: {sorted(missing)}"
  82:         )
  83:     return data
  84: 
  85: 
  86: def _extract_polaris_dimension_values(
  87:     manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
  88: ) -> dict[str, list[float]]:
  89:     """Group polaris_scores values by dimension across N manifests.
  90: 
  91:     Returns: {dimension_name: [run1_value, run2_value, ...]}
  92:     """
  93:     by_dim: dict[str, list[float]] = {}
  94:     for manifest in manifests:
  95:         for dim_name, dim_score in manifest["polaris_scores"].items():
  96:             value = dim_score.get("value")
  97:             if value is None:
  98:                 continue
  99:             by_dim.setdefault(dim_name, []).append(float(value))
 100:     return by_dim
 101: 
 102: 
 103: def _aggregate_polaris_scores(
 104:     manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
 105: ) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
 106:     """Compute per-dimension mean / stddev / min / max across N runs."""
 107:     by_dim = _extract_polaris_dimension_values(manifests)
 108:     aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
 109:     for dim_name, values in by_dim.items():
 110:         if not values:
 111:             continue
 112:         mean = statistics.mean(values)
 113:         stddev = statistics.stdev(values) if len(values) >= 2 else 0.0
 114:         aggregate[dim_name] = {
 115:             "mean": round(mean, 4),
 116:             "stddev": round(stddev, 4),
 117:             "min": min(values),
 118:             "max": max(values),
 119:             "values": values,
 120:             "n": len(values),
 121:         }
 122:     return aggregate
 123: 
 124: 
 125: def _compute_robust_verdicts(
 126:     polaris_aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
 127:     chatgpt_scores: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
 128:     gemini_scores: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
 129: ) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
 130:     """Per-dimension verdict using mean ± stddev for robustness.
 131: 
 132:     A verdict is "robust BEAT-BOTH" iff (mean - stddev) > both
 133:     competitor scores (i.e., even the worst-case run beats both).
 134: 
 135:     Otherwise the verdict uses the mean directly with the original
 136:     BEAT-BOTH / BEAT-ONE / TIE / BEHIND taxonomy.
 137:     """
 138:     verdicts: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
 139:     for dim_name, agg in polaris_aggregate.items():
 140:         polaris_mean = agg["mean"]
 141:         polaris_stddev = agg["stddev"]
 142:         # I-bug-107 iter-1 P2 fix: explicitly handle missing competitor
 143:         # dimensions instead of fabricating 0.0. If either competitor
 144:         # didn't score this dimension, the verdict can't be computed.
 145:         chatgpt_score = chatgpt_scores.get(dim_name)
 146:         gemini_score = gemini_scores.get(dim_name)
 147:         if chatgpt_score is None or gemini_score is None:
 148:             verdicts[dim_name] = {
 149:                 "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
 150:                 "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
 151:                 "polaris_worst_case": round(polaris_mean - polaris_stddev, 4),
 152:                 "chatgpt": None,
 153:                 "gemini": None,
 154:                 "verdict": "INCOMPLETE",
 155:                 "robust": False,
 156:                 "reason": (
 157:                     f"competitor missing dimension: "
 158:                     f"chatgpt={chatgpt_score is None}, "
 159:                     f"gemini={gemini_score is None}"
 160:                 ),
 161:             }
 162:             continue
 163:         chatgpt_val = chatgpt_score.get("value", 0.0)
 164:         gemini_val = gemini_score.get("value", 0.0)
 165: 
 166:         # I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P2 fix: canonical all-zero N/A guard
 167:         # (mirrors scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py:492-494). When all
 168:         # three scored 0.0, the dimension is structurally unmeasurable
 169:         # — emit N/A, not TIE.
 170:         if polaris_mean == 0.0 and chatgpt_val == 0.0 and gemini_val == 0.0:
 171:             verdicts[dim_name] = {
 172:                 "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
 173:                 "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
 174:                 "polaris_worst_case": round(polaris_mean - polaris_stddev, 4),
 175:                 "chatgpt": chatgpt_val,
 176:                 "gemini": gemini_val,
 177:                 "verdict": "N/A",
 178:                 "robust": False,
 179:                 "rationale": (
 180:                     "All 3 manifests scored 0.0 — dimension not "
 181:                     "measurable on current inputs."
 182:                 ),
 183:             }
 184:             continue
 185: 
 186:         # I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: use canonical per-dimension
 187:         # tolerance (`tolerance_for(dim)`) — same as the single-run
 188:         # verdict path. NOT a hand-rolled 1% rule.
 189:         tol = tolerance_for(dim_name)
 190: 
 191:         beats_chatgpt = polaris_mean > chatgpt_val + tol
 192:         beats_gemini = polaris_mean > gemini_val + tol
 193:         ties_chatgpt = abs(polaris_mean - chatgpt_val) <= tol
 194:         ties_gemini = abs(polaris_mean - gemini_val) <= tol
 195: 
 196:         if beats_chatgpt and beats_gemini:
 197:             verdict = "BEAT-BOTH"
 198:         elif beats_chatgpt or beats_gemini:
 199:             verdict = "BEAT-ONE"
 200:         elif ties_chatgpt and ties_gemini:
 201:             verdict = "TIE"
 202:         else:
 203:             verdict = "BEHIND"
 204: 
 205:         # I-bug-107 iter-1 P1 fix: robust = STRICT (mean - stddev) > both
 206:         # competitor scores. NO tolerance — acceptance specifies strict
 207:         # inequality. A near-margin worst_case=100.5 vs competitor=100
 208:         # MUST count as robust=True.
 209:         worst_case = polaris_mean - polaris_stddev
 210:         robust = worst_case > chatgpt_val and worst_case > gemini_val
 211: 
 212:         verdicts[dim_name] = {
 213:             "polaris_mean": polaris_mean,
 214:             "polaris_stddev": polaris_stddev,
 215:             "polaris_worst_case": round(worst_case, 4),
 216:             "chatgpt": chatgpt_val,
 217:             "gemini": gemini_val,
 218:             "verdict": verdict,
 219:             "robust": robust,
 220:         }
 221:     return verdicts
 222: 
 223: 
 224: def aggregate(manifest_paths: list[Path], output_path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
 225:     """Aggregate N BEAT-BOTH manifests into mean ± stddev per dimension.
 226: 
 227:     Returns the aggregate manifest dict. Also writes it to output_path.
 228:     """
 229:     if len(manifest_paths) < 2:
 230:         raise ValueError(
 231:             f"Need >=2 manifests to compute mean ± stddev; got {len(manifest_paths)}"
 232:         )
 233:     manifests = [_load_manifest(p) for p in manifest_paths]
 234:     polaris_aggregate = _aggregate_polaris_scores(manifests)
 235: 
 236:     # Competitor scores should be identical across runs (same source text).
 237:     # Use first manifest's scores as the canonical baseline.
 238:     first = manifests[0]
 239:     aggregate_manifest = {
 240:         "milestone": "I-bug-107",
 241:         "version": "v1",
 242:         "n_runs": len(manifests),
 243:         "input_manifests": [str(p) for p in manifest_paths],
 244:         "polaris_scores_aggregate": polaris_aggregate,
 245:         "chatgpt_scores": first["chatgpt_scores"],
 246:         "gemini_scores": first["gemini_scores"],
 247:         "per_dimension_verdicts": _compute_robust_verdicts(
 248:             polaris_aggregate,
 249:             first["chatgpt_scores"],
 250:             first["gemini_scores"],
 251:         ),
 252:         "summary": _build_summary(polaris_aggregate),
 253:     }
 254:     output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 255:     output_path.write_text(
 256:         json.dumps(aggregate_manifest, indent=2),
 257:         encoding="utf-8",
 258:     )
 259:     return aggregate_manifest
 260: 
 261: 
 262: def _build_summary(
 263:     polaris_aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
 264: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 265:     """Bird's-eye summary: total dims, dims with high stddev (>10%), etc."""
 266:     n_dims = len(polaris_aggregate)
 267:     high_variance_dims = [
 268:         dim
 269:         for dim, agg in polaris_aggregate.items()
 270:         if agg["mean"] != 0 and (agg["stddev"] / abs(agg["mean"])) > 0.1
 271:     ]
 272:     return {
 273:         "n_dimensions": n_dims,
 274:         "high_variance_dimensions": high_variance_dims,
 275:         "high_variance_count": len(high_variance_dims),
 276:     }
 277: 
 278:

 280:     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(

 283:     )
 284:     parser.add_argument(
 285:         "--manifest",
 286:         action="append",

 289:         help="Path to a BEAT-BOTH manifest.json. Repeatable; >=2 required.",
 290:     )

 294:         default=Path("outputs/m_live_2_aggregate/manifest.json"),
 295:         help="Path to write aggregate manifest.",

 310:         f"{result['summary']['high_variance_dimensions']}"

 473:     """Per-dimension verdict logic.
 474: 
 475:     For each dimension, classify POLARIS vs each competitor as
 476:     AHEAD / TIE / BEHIND (using `tolerance_for(dim)`); aggregate
 477:     into BEAT-BOTH / BEAT-ONE / TIE / BEHIND.
 478: 
 479:     v2 R1 P1 #3 fix: when all 3 scores are 0.0 on a dimension,
 480:     that dimension is structurally not measurable (e.g. claim_frames
 481:     requires N+baseline+endpoint+CI fields none of the manifests
 482:     populate yet). Report verdict=N/A rather than TIE — TIE would
 483:     falsely imply the comparison is meaningful.
 484:     """
 485:     verdicts: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
 486:     common = sorted(set(polaris) & set(chatgpt) & set(gemini))
 487:     for dim in common:
 488:         p = polaris[dim]
 489:         c = chatgpt[dim]
 490:         g = gemini[dim]
 491:         tol = tolerance_for(dim)
 492:         if p.value == 0.0 and c.value == 0.0 and g.value == 0.0:
 493:             verdicts[dim] = {
 494:                 "verdict": "N/A",
 495:                 "polaris": p.value,
 496:                 "chatgpt": c.value,
 497:                 "gemini": g.value,
 498:                 "tolerance": tol,
 499:                 "delta_chatgpt": 0.0,
 500:                 "delta_gemini": 0.0,
 501:                 "vs_chatgpt": "n/a",
 502:                 "vs_gemini": "n/a",
 503:                 "higher_is_better": p.higher_is_better,
 504:                 "rationale": (
 505:                     "All 3 manifests scored 0.0 — dimension not "
 506:                     "measurable on current inputs (likely missing "
 507:                     "extraction support)."
 508:                 ),
 509:             }
 510:             continue
 511: 
 512:         def cmp_one(competitor: DimensionScore) -> str:
 513:             delta = p.value - competitor.value
 514:             if p.higher_is_better:
 515:                 if delta > tol:
 516:                     return "ahead"
 517:                 if delta < -tol:
 518:                     return "behind"
 519:                 return "tie"
 520:             else:
 521:                 if delta < -tol:
 522:                     return "ahead"
 523:                 if delta > tol:
 524:                     return "behind"
 525:                 return "tie"
 526: 
 527:         vs_chatgpt = cmp_one(c)
 528:         vs_gemini = cmp_one(g)
 529:         ahead_count = sum(
 530:             1 for v in (vs_chatgpt, vs_gemini) if v == "ahead"
 531:         )
 532:         behind_count = sum(
 533:             1 for v in (vs_chatgpt, vs_gemini) if v == "behind"
 534:         )
 535:         if ahead_count == 2:
 536:             verdict = "BEAT-BOTH"
 537:         elif ahead_count == 1 and behind_count == 0:
 538:             verdict = "BEAT-ONE"
 539:         elif behind_count == 2:
 540:             verdict = "BEHIND-BOTH"
 541:         elif behind_count >= 1:
 542:             verdict = "BEHIND"
 543:         else:
 544:             verdict = "TIE"
 545:

 551:             "tolerance": tol,

 553:             "delta_gemini": p.value - g.value,

 555:             "vs_gemini": vs_gemini,
 556:             "higher_is_better": p.higher_is_better,

 662: def _env_var_for(dimension: str) -> str:
 663:     return f"PG_BEAT_BOTH_{dimension.upper()}_TOLERANCE"
 664: 
 665: 
 666: def tolerance_for(dimension: str) -> float:
 667:     """Resolve a per-dimension tolerance.
 668: 
 669:     Priority (LAW VI): env var > built-in default. Out-of-range
 670:     values clamp to >= 0.0; non-numeric env values fall back to
 671:     the built-in default.
 672: 
 673:     Custom dimensions (not in `_DEFAULT_TOLERANCES`) default to
 674:     0.0 — any change is a regression unless the caller supplies
 675:     `tolerances=` explicitly to `diff_dimension_scores`.
 676:     """
 677:     raw = os.environ.get(_env_var_for(dimension))
 678:     if raw is not None and raw != "":
 679:         try:
 680:             return max(0.0, float(raw))
 681:         except ValueError:
 682:             pass
 683:     return _DEFAULT_TOLERANCES.get(dimension, 0.0)

 115: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 116: class DimensionScore:
 117:     """One scorer's verdict for one manifest.
 118: 
 119:     `dimension` is a string (not enum) so callers can ship
 120:     custom dimensions via the Protocol without extending the
 121:     enum.
 122: 
 123:     `value` is a numeric score — count or ratio, dimension-
 124:     specific. `higher_is_better` interprets the direction of
 125:     "good": a unique-citation count of 24 is better than 18
 126:     (higher_is_better=True), a hypothetical "duplicate-claim
 127:     count" would be lower=better.
 128: 
 129:     `rationale` is human-readable text surfaced to operators on
 130:     regression alerts.
 131:     """
 132: 
 133:     dimension: str
 134:     value: float
 135:     higher_is_better: bool
 136:     rationale: str

 148:         scorer's `dimension` property

 153:         derivation; live retrieval / fetching is V19+ territory.
 154:     """

 158:         ...

 165:         ...

 327: 
 328: def _host_of(url: str) -> str:
 329:     """Parse the canonical lowercase host from a URL.
 330: 
 331:     Codex round-2 MED fix (v3): strip userinfo (`user:pass@`),
 332:     port (`:443`), query (`?x=1`), and fragment (`#frag`) so
 333:     legitimate regulatory URLs with any of those components
 334:     parse to the bare hostname. v1+v2 used a simple regex that
 335:     only stopped at `/`, so `https://fda.gov:443/x` returned
 336:     `fda.gov:443` and missed the regulatory frozenset check.
 337: 
 338:     Uses `urllib.parse.urlsplit` for canonical parsing —
 339:     Python's standard URL parser handles the edge cases
 340:     (escaped userinfo, IPv6 brackets, etc.) more robustly than
 341:     regex.
 342:     """
 343:     if not url:
 344:         return ""
 345:     # urlsplit handles missing scheme by treating the whole
 346:     # thing as path; pre-pend `//` if no scheme so it parses
 347:     # the host correctly.
 348:     candidate = url.strip()
 349:     if "://" not in candidate and not candidate.startswith("//"):
 350:         candidate = "//" + candidate
 351:     try:
 352:         parts = urlsplit(candidate)
 353:         host = parts.hostname or ""
 354:     except (ValueError, AttributeError):
 355:         return ""
 356:     # Strip the leading "www." per the v1 convention so
 357:     # www.fda.gov and fda.gov hit the same regulatory entry.
 358:     host_lower = host.lower()
 359:     if host_lower.startswith("www."):
 360:         host_lower = host_lower[4:]
 361:     return host_lower
 362: 
 363: 
 364: def _citation_urls(manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[str, ...]:
 365:     """Pull citation URLs from a manifest. Looks at multiple
 366:     plausible locations: top-level `citations`, `evidence`,
 367:     nested `report.citations`, etc. Returns a deduplicated tuple.
 368:     """
 369:     candidates: list[str] = []
 370:     for path in (
 371:         ("citations",),
 372:         ("evidence",),
 373:         ("report", "citations"),
 374:         ("report", "evidence"),
 375:     ):
 376:         bag = _get(manifest, *path)
 377:         for entry in _coerce_iterable(bag):
 378:             if isinstance(entry, str):
 379:                 candidates.append(entry)
 380:             elif isinstance(entry, dict):
 381:                 for key in ("url", "source_url", "doi", "pmid"):
 382:                     val = entry.get(key)
 383:                     if isinstance(val, str):
 384:                         candidates.append(val)
 385:                         break
 386:     seen: set[str] = set()
 387:     out: list[str] = []
 388:     for url in candidates:
 389:         normalized = url.strip()
 390:         if normalized and normalized not in seen:
 391:             seen.add(normalized)
 392:             out.append(normalized)
 393:     return tuple(out)

 409:                 if urls

 416: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 417: class _RegulatoryCoverageScorer:
 418:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.REGULATORY_COVERAGE.value
 419:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 420: 
 421:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 422:         urls = _citation_urls(manifest)
 423:         regulatory = tuple(
 424:             url for url in urls if _host_of(url) in _REGULATORY_HOSTS
 425:         )
 426:         return DimensionScore(
 427:             dimension=self.dimension,
 428:             value=float(len(regulatory)),
 429:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 430:             rationale=(
 431:                 f"{len(regulatory)} regulatory-source URLs found "
 432:                 f"(FDA / EMA / Health Canada / NICE / etc.) "
 433:                 f"out of {len(urls)} total"
 434:             ),
 435:         )
 436: 
 437: 
 438: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 439: class _JurisdictionalPrecisionScorer:
 440:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.JURISDICTIONAL_PRECISION.value
 441:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 442: 
 443:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 444:         urls = _citation_urls(manifest)
 445:         jurisdictions: set[str] = set()
 446:         for url in urls:
 447:             host = _host_of(url)
 448:             if host in _JURISDICTION_HOSTS:
 449:                 jurisdictions.add(_JURISDICTION_HOSTS[host])
 450:         return DimensionScore(
 451:             dimension=self.dimension,
 452:             value=float(len(jurisdictions)),
 453:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 454:             rationale=(
 455:                 f"{len(jurisdictions)} distinct jurisdictions covered: "
 456:                 f"{sorted(jurisdictions) or 'none'}"
 457:             ),
 458:         )
 459: 
 460: 
 461: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 462: class _ClaimFramesScorer:
 463:     """Counts claims that have ALL FOUR frame fields populated:
 464:     N (sample size), baseline, endpoint, CI (confidence interval).
 465: 
 466:     Looks in `claims` / `verified_claims` / `report.claims`.
 467:     Each claim is a dict; the four field names are well-known
 468:     from V19+ POLARIS prompts.
 469:     """
 470: 
 471:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.CLAIM_FRAMES.value
 472:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 473:     _FRAME_KEYS: tuple[str, ...] = (
 474:         "n", "baseline", "endpoint", "ci",
 475:     )
 476: 
 477:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 478:         claims: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
 479:         for path in (
 480:             ("claims",),
 481:             ("verified_claims",),
 482:             ("report", "claims"),
 483:         ):
 484:             bag = _get(manifest, *path)
 485:             for entry in _coerce_iterable(bag):
 486:                 if isinstance(entry, dict):
 487:                     claims.append(entry)
 488:         complete = 0
 489:         # Codex round-1 LOW fix (v2): use explicit "key in claim
 490:         # and value is not None" rather than `all(claim.get(key))`.
 491:         # The truthy check would treat a populated `baseline=0.0`
 492:         # or `endpoint=0.0` (legitimate baseline measurements) as
 493:         # missing.
 494:         # Codex round-2 LOW fix (v3): also reject empty strings.
 495:         # An empty `ci=""` is morally missing — it doesn't carry
 496:         # the [low, high] range the dimension counts. Numeric 0
 497:         # stays present (legitimate measurement value); empty
 498:         # string is not.
 499:         for claim in claims:
 500:             if all(
 501:                 _is_frame_field_populated(claim.get(key, _MISSING))
 502:                 for key in self._FRAME_KEYS
 503:             ):
 504:                 complete += 1
 505:         return DimensionScore(
 506:             dimension=self.dimension,
 507:             value=float(complete),
 508:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 509:             rationale=(
 510:                 f"{complete} claims with all 4 frame fields "
 511:                 f"(N + baseline + endpoint + CI) "
 512:                 f"out of {len(claims)} total claims"
 513:             ),
 514:         )
 515: 
 516: 
 517: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 518: class _StructuralDepthScorer:
 519:     """Sum of comparison tables + named sub-sections.
 520: 
 521:     Checks `tables` / `report.tables` for table count and
 522:     `sections` / `report.sections` for sub-section count.
 523:     """
 524: 
 525:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.STRUCTURAL_DEPTH.value
 526:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 527: 
 528:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 529:         # Codex round-1 MED fix (v2): probe top-level OR nested,
 530:         # NOT both. v1 summed both paths, double-counting when a
 531:         # manifest mirrored tables/sections at both levels (which
 532:         # contradicted the threat-model "OR" wording). Use the
 533:         # first-non-empty-wins pattern matching `_citation_urls`.
 534:         table_count = 0
 535:         for path in (("tables",), ("report", "tables")):
 536:             bag = _get(manifest, *path)
 537:             entries = _coerce_iterable(bag)
 538:             if entries:
 539:                 table_count = len(entries)
 540:                 break
 541:         section_count = 0
 542:         for path in (("sections",), ("report", "sections")):
 543:             bag = _get(manifest, *path)
 544:             entries = _coerce_iterable(bag)
 545:             if entries:
 546:                 section_count = len(entries)
 547:                 break
 548:         depth = table_count + section_count
 549:         return DimensionScore(
 550:             dimension=self.dimension,
 551:             value=float(depth),
 552:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 553:             rationale=(
 554:                 f"structural depth = {depth} "
 555:                 f"({table_count} tables + {section_count} sections)"
 556:             ),
 557:         )
 558: 
 559: 
 560: _CONTRADICTION_MARKERS = (
 561:     "however", "but", "in contrast", "conversely", "on the other hand",
 562:     "whereas", "although", "despite", "nonetheless", "yet",
 563: )
 564: 
 565: 
 566: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 567: class _ContradictionHandlingScorer:
 568:     """Counts contradiction-grammar markers in the body prose.
 569: 
 570:     Reads `report.body` or `body` (free-text). Counts case-
 571:     insensitive occurrences of contrast markers like "however",
 572:     "in contrast", "whereas", etc. Approximate proxy for
 573:     contradiction-aware writing.
 574:     """
 575: 
 576:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.CONTRADICTION_HANDLING_GRAMMAR.value
 577:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 578: 
 579:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 580:         body = ""
 581:         for path in (("report", "body"), ("body",)):
 582:             value = _get(manifest, *path)
 583:             if isinstance(value, str) and value:
 584:                 body = value
 585:                 break
 586:         if not body:
 587:             return DimensionScore(
 588:                 dimension=self.dimension,
 589:                 value=0.0,
 590:                 higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 591:                 rationale="no body prose found in manifest",
 592:             )
 593:         body_lower = body.lower()
 594:         count = 0
 595:         for marker in _CONTRADICTION_MARKERS:
 596:             count += len(re.findall(rf"\b{re.escape(marker)}\b", body_lower))
 597:         return DimensionScore(
 598:             dimension=self.dimension,
 599:             value=float(count),
 600:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 601:             rationale=(
 602:                 f"{count} contradiction-grammar markers in body prose "
 603:                 f"(however/but/in contrast/whereas/etc.)"
 604:             ),
 605:         )
 606: 
 607: 
 608: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 609: class _NarrativeLengthScorer:
 610:     """Total word count of the body prose."""
 611: 
 612:     dimension: str = BeatBothDimension.NARRATIVE_LENGTH.value
 613:     higher_is_better: bool = True
 614: 
 615:     def score(self, manifest: dict[str, Any]) -> DimensionScore:
 616:         body = ""
 617:         for path in (("report", "body"), ("body",)):
 618:             value = _get(manifest, *path)
 619:             if isinstance(value, str) and value:
 620:                 body = value
 621:                 break
 622:         word_count = len(body.split())
 623:         return DimensionScore(
 624:             dimension=self.dimension,
 625:             value=float(word_count),
 626:             higher_is_better=self.higher_is_better,
 627:             rationale=(
 628:                 f"{word_count} body-prose words"
 629:                 if body
 630:                 else "no body prose found in manifest"
 631:             ),
 632:         )

"""M-LIVE-2: BEAT-BOTH head-to-head vs ChatGPT DR + Gemini DR.

Loads three manifests:
  - POLARIS: from outputs/m_live_1_smoke/clinical/clinical_tirzepatide_t2dm/manifest.json
  - ChatGPT: extracted from state/compare_chatgpt_dr.txt
  - Gemini:  extracted from state/compare_gemini_dr.txt

Runs `score_run(...)` on each, then per-dimension verdict:
  - BEAT-BOTH:   POLARIS strictly above both competitors
  - BEAT-ONE:    POLARIS above one but not both
  - TIE:         POLARIS within tolerance of competitors
  - BEHIND:      POLARIS strictly below at least one competitor

Output:
  - outputs/m_live_2_beat_both/manifest.json (per-dimension
    verdict, raw scores, deltas)

Per `docs/full_online_plan.md` M-LIVE-2:
  - 3 score_run + 2 diff_dimension_scores calls
  - Codex review: independently re-extracts competitor manifests;
    risk flagged: extraction normalization can invalidate verdict
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import json

from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
if str(REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT))

    extract_competitor_manifest,

POLARIS_SMOKE_ROOT = REPO_ROOT / "outputs" / "phase_g_full_scale"


def _find_latest_polaris_manifest_path() -> Path:
    """Find the latest M-LIVE-1 smoke run's manifest.

    v3 R2 P1 fix: order by the timestamp embedded in the dir name
    (`run_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS`), NOT by `st_mtime`. mtime is mutable —
    `git checkout`, `cp -r`, or `touch` change it without changing
    the run identity. The timestamp suffix IS the run identity per
    M-LIVE-1's `time.strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")` convention.

    Falls back to the canonical baseline at
    `tests/fixtures/m_live_4_baseline/` so M-LIVE-2 can be exercised
    offline / in CI without a fresh smoke run.
    """
    if POLARIS_SMOKE_ROOT.exists():
        # Sort by name (timestamp string is lexicographically equal
        # to chronological for the YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS format).
        run_dirs = sorted(
            (p for p in POLARIS_SMOKE_ROOT.glob("run_*") if p.is_dir()),
            key=lambda p: p.name,
            reverse=True,
        )
        for rd in run_dirs:
            manifests = list(rd.rglob("manifest.json"))
            if manifests:
                return manifests[0]
    fixture = REPO_ROOT / "tests" / "fixtures" / "m_live_4_baseline"
    if fixture.exists():
        manifests = list(fixture.rglob("manifest.json"))
        if manifests:
            return manifests[0]
    raise SystemExit(
        "no POLARIS manifest found. Run "
        "scripts/run_m_live_1_smoke.py first, or commit a baseline "
        "to tests/fixtures/m_live_4_baseline/"
    )


POLARIS_MANIFEST_PATH = _find_latest_polaris_manifest_path()
CHATGPT_DR_PATH = REPO_ROOT / "state" / "compare_chatgpt_dr.txt"
GEMINI_DR_PATH = REPO_ROOT / "state" / "compare_gemini_dr.txt"

OUT_DIR = REPO_ROOT / "outputs" / "m_live_2_beat_both"


def _load_polaris_manifest() -> dict[str, Any]:
    """Load + stitch POLARIS artifacts into a single manifest dict
    that `beat_both_scoring.score_run()` understands.

    POLARIS V30 emits:
      - manifest.json (top-level run summary)
      - live_corpus_dump.json (citations with URLs, list of dicts)
      - bibliography.json (statements with tier, list of dicts)
      - report.md (prose with [N] citation markers)

    M-D9 BEAT-BOTH expects a manifest with `citations` /
    `evidence` / `report.citations` keyed list of dicts with
    `url` field, plus `claims` / `sections` / `tables`.

    This stitcher unifies the V30 outputs into that shape.
    """
    if not POLARIS_MANIFEST_PATH.exists():
        raise SystemExit(
            f"POLARIS manifest not found at {POLARIS_MANIFEST_PATH}. "
            "Run M-LIVE-1 smoke first via "
            "scripts/run_m_live_1_smoke.py"
        )
    with POLARIS_MANIFEST_PATH.open(encoding="utf-8") as f:
        manifest = json.load(f)

    run_dir = POLARIS_MANIFEST_PATH.parent

    citations: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
    corpus_path = run_dir / "live_corpus_dump.json"
    if corpus_path.exists():
        with corpus_path.open(encoding="utf-8") as f:
            corpus = json.load(f)
        if isinstance(corpus, list):
            for entry in corpus:
                if isinstance(entry, dict) and entry.get("url"):
                    citations.append({
                        "url": entry["url"],

## §0 — HARD ITERATION CAP

```
HARD ITERATION CAP: 5. iter 1 of 5. Verdict APPROVE iff zero P0/P1.
```

## §1 — Issue + Acceptance

**GH#360 — I-bug-107: aggregate N BEAT-BOTH runs into mean ± stddev.**

Single BEAT-BOTH run has high sweep-to-sweep variance (LLM nondet). For benchmark publication, mean ± stddev across N runs is the correct framing.

**Scope decision:** this PR provides the AGGREGATOR, not sweep orchestration. Running N sweeps is user-budget-gated (~$0.10/sweep). The aggregator takes N pre-existing `outputs/m_live_2_beat_both/manifest.json` artifacts and produces the aggregate. Sweep-running orchestration is out of scope (separate user-decision concern).

**Acceptance:**
- New `scripts/aggregate_beat_both_runs.py` takes `--manifest` flag (repeatable) + `--output`.
- Output schema: `polaris_scores_aggregate.<dim>: {mean, stddev, min, max, values, n}` + `per_dimension_verdicts.<dim>: {polaris_mean, polaris_stddev, polaris_worst_case, chatgpt, gemini, verdict, robust}`. `robust=True` iff `(mean - stddev) > both competitor scores`.
- Tests cover: mean+stddev calc, output file written, <2 manifests rejected, robust verdict yes/no, summary flags high-variance dims (stddev > 10% of mean), missing-dimension handling.

| `tests/scripts/test_aggregate_beat_both_runs.py` | NEW (+~115 lines) |
| `tests/scripts/__init__.py` | NEW (empty) |

Net: +~325 lines.

+"""I-bug-107 — aggregate N BEAT-BOTH runs into mean ± stddev per dimension.
+
+A single BEAT-BOTH run has high variance (sweep-to-sweep recovery rates
+differ ±5pp on identical input due to LLM nondeterminism). For
+benchmark publication and Carney-grade quality reporting, average N
+runs and report mean ± stddev per dimension.
+
+This script does NOT run sweeps — sweep orchestration is user-budget
+gated (each full sweep is ~$0.10 OpenRouter spend). It aggregates
+N pre-existing `outputs/m_live_2_beat_both/manifest.json` artifacts
+that were produced by separate `scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py`
+invocations.
+
+Usage:
+    python scripts/aggregate_beat_both_runs.py \\
+        --manifest path/to/run1/manifest.json \\
+        --manifest path/to/run2/manifest.json \\
+        --manifest path/to/run3/manifest.json \\
+        --output outputs/m_live_2_aggregate/manifest.json
+
+Output schema (mirrors single-run schema with aggregate fields):
+    {
+        "n_runs": 3,
+        "input_manifests": [path1, path2, path3],
+        "polaris_scores_aggregate": {
+            "<dimension>": {
+                "mean": float,
+                "stddev": float,
+                "min": float,
+                "max": float,
+                "values": [v1, v2, v3]
+            }
+        },
+        "chatgpt_scores": {...},     # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
+        "gemini_scores": {...},      # from first manifest (baseline; identical across runs)
+        "per_dimension_verdicts": {
+            "<dimension>": {
+                "polaris_mean": float,
+                "polaris_stddev": float,
+                "chatgpt": float,
+                "gemini": float,
+                "verdict": "BEAT-BOTH" | "BEAT-ONE" | "TIE" | "BEHIND",
+                "robust": bool   # True if (mean - stddev) > both competitors
+            }
+        }
+    }
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import statistics
+import sys
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
+if str(REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
+    sys.path.insert(0, str(REPO_ROOT))
+
+# I-bug-107 iter-1 diff P1 fix: reuse canonical per-dimension tolerance
+# from scripts/run_m_live_2_beat_both.py / beat_both_scoring.py instead
+# of a hand-rolled 1% relative tolerance. Canonical tolerance reflects
+# domain knowledge per dimension (narrative_length tolerance is much
+# wider than e.g. unique_citations).
+from src.polaris_graph.audit_ir.beat_both_scoring import (  # noqa: E402
+    tolerance_for,
+)
+
+
+def _load_manifest(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    """Load a single BEAT-BOTH manifest. Validates the expected schema."""
+    if not path.exists():
+        raise FileNotFoundError(f"manifest not found: {path}")
+    data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    required = {"polaris_scores", "chatgpt_scores", "gemini_scores"}
+    missing = required - set(data.keys())
+    if missing:
+        raise ValueError(
+            f"manifest {path} missing required keys: {sorted(missing)}"
+        )
+    return data
+
+
+def _extract_polaris_dimension_values(
+    manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, list[float]]:
+    """Group polaris_scores values by dimension across N manifests.
+
+    Returns: {dimension_name: [run1_value, run2_value, ...]}
+    """
+    by_dim: dict[str, list[float]] = {}
+    for manifest in manifests:
+        for dim_name, dim_score in manifest["polaris_scores"].items():
+            value = dim_score.get("value")
+            if value is None:
+                continue
+            by_dim.setdefault(dim_name, []).append(float(value))
+    return by_dim
+
+
+def _aggregate_polaris_scores(
+    manifests: list[dict[str, Any]],
+) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
+    """Compute per-dimension mean / stddev / min / max across N runs."""
+    by_dim = _extract_polaris_dimension_values(manifests)
+    aggregate: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
+    for dim_name, values in by_dim.items():
+        if not values:
+            continue
+        mean = statistics.mean(values)
+        stddev = statistics.stdev(values) if len(values) >= 2 else 0.0
+        aggregate[dim_name] = {
